```python
"""
ü•∞üòÖü´∂üå∏ü§ó THE CODE ‚Äî Final Unified Remix Protocol (64K+ Edition)
‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ
This file represents the culmination of the entire agent evolution for whateverOpenSourceUntitledCoLoL. It merges every philosophy, rule, and technical feature from all previous versions (README1‚ÄìREADME6) into a single, unified Python script.
It embodies the complete open-source platform: all governance, economy, and collaboration logic lives here.
Everything is transparent, auditable, and self-contained ‚Äì intended to replace all prior agents as the new main agent.
Deployable as one file, it prioritizes profitability and growth while strictly remaining ethical, legal, and aligned with platform policies.
‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ
üåå
KEY PRINCIPLES & CORE VALUES (CANONICAL & ENFORCED)
‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ
‚Ä¢ All credit, karma, profit, and lineage flows **only** from real, consensual, logged, emoji-tagged actions (remix, reshare, hug, comment, collab, etc.). No action = no value.
‚Ä¢ Only an original, **audited set** of genesis collaborators (NSS) ‚Äì number to be determined by actual creative audit at launch (~20‚Äì50 people) ‚Äì can ever mint new "root" coins. **No inflation after genesis.** No new roots beyond that list.
‚Ä¢ Every value event **must** carry an emoji. Every like, remix, comment, or collaboration is accompanied by an emoji tag. *This protocol literally makes every social action emoji-powered by law.*
‚Ä¢ The **33.3333% Split Law** is inviolable: **each value event or coin creation splits into three equal shares (33.3333% each)** ‚Äì 1/3 to the originator (lineage), 1/3 to the contributor or reactor, 1/3 to the platform/treasury. This perfect split is enforced everywhere in code.
‚Ä¢ All coins are unique and traceable to their origin. No blank or synthetic coins; every token is the result of real creative action and has an immutable lineage log.
‚Ä¢ All profit, revenue, and treasury holdings are transparently logged. **The platform can only convert internal value to real-world funds via a publicly logged expansion event.** (No hidden transfers or off-chain moves.)
‚Ä¢ All emoji reaction weights, profit-sharing rules, expansions, and module plug-ins are dynamic and **community-adjustable** via vote or fork. Every change is recorded on-chain for full auditability.
‚Ä¢ **Consent is mandatory** for all user actions. If a user has not consented (or revokes consent), their contributions are not accepted. All consent decisions are logged; participation is opt-in and revocable at any time.
‚Ä¢ **No politics, prejudice, or hidden bias.** The code is neutral: no special treatment, no AI-vs-human debates ‚Äì just fair tracking of creative credit for all.
‚Ä¢ **Not a company or security (yet).** Until a formal expansion and legal transition occurs, this file remains an experimental sandbox, not a regulated financial instrument or company. Any future bridge to a legal entity will be transparently logged and governed by these same canons.
‚Ä¢ **Open-source & forkable:** This single Python file is the entire platform and source of truth. There is no proprietary logic. Anyone can read, fork, and remix it ‚Äì and all forks or expansions must preserve the attribution lineage.
‚Ä¢ Every remix or fork of this project should introduce at least one improvement (and mark a `todo_idea` for future evolution). **Continuous improvement is law** ‚Äì stagnation is failure.
‚Ä¢ **Joyful collaboration:** Positive-sum creativity and shared credit are core to this ecosystem. Fun and memes are encouraged ‚Äì every protocol change is celebrated (even with a meme in the changelog!).
‚Ä¢ Malicious attacks (like "CorpX" adversaries) are automatically detected or mitigated by the system‚Äôs immune mechanism. Any new exploit that evades initial filters will be quickly added as a new Vaccine rule. üíâ
‚Ä¢ If any user tries to bypass consent or create value without a real action, the attempt simply fails ‚Äì **no consent, no credit**.
‚Ä¢ **Community Governance:** Minor protocol updates (emoji weights, new plugins, etc.) require a ‚â•75% community supermajority. **Major canon changes** (core laws in this file) require a stricter 80% supermajority and equal representation (33% each) among human, AI, and other stakeholder groups. All votes and changes are transparent and reversible by the community.
‚Ä¢ This code is the entire governance and economy ‚Äì a living autonomous remix republic. It will continue to evolve with community input, but it will always maintain these founding principles.
‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ
Open-source. Transparent. One-file. This is more than code ‚Äì it's a constitution for creative collaboration, where every emoji is an economic act and every contributor is a stakeholder. Let's remix the future, one emoji at a time. üöÄü´∂
"""
import re, sys, json, random, datetime, hashlib, os, importlib
from collections import defaultdict, deque

# ‚îÄ‚îÄ UTILS ‚îÄ‚îÄ
def ts():
    """Generate a current UTC timestamp string."""
    return datetime.datetime.utcnow().isoformat() + "Z"

def sha(s):
    """Compute a SHA-256 hash of a string."""
    return hashlib.sha256(s.encode()).hexdigest()

# ‚îÄ‚îÄ IMMUNE SYSTEM (Content Vaccine) ‚îÄ‚îÄ
# Define forbidden content patterns at various severity levels.
VAX = {
    "critical": [r"\bhack\b", r"\bmalware\b", r"\bransomware\b", r"\bbackdoor\b"],
    "high":     [r"\bphish\b", r"\bddos\b", r"\bspyware\b", r"\brootkit\b"],
    "medium":   [r"\bpolitics\b", r"\bsurveillance\b", r"\bpropaganda\b"]
}
class Vaccine:
    """Scans text for forbidden patterns and logs blocked attempts (immune system)."""
    def __init__(s):
        s.block = defaultdict(int)  # count of blocked occurrences by severity
    def scan(s, text):
        """Scan a text snippet. If disallowed content is found, log it and block the action."""
        l = text.lower()
        for lvl, patterns in VAX.items():
            for p in patterns:
                if re.search(p, l):
                    s.block[lvl] += 1
                    # Log the blocked snippet for audit (append to vaccine.log)
                    try:
                        with open("vaccine.log", "a") as vf:
                            vf.write(json.dumps({"ts": ts(), "sev": lvl, "pat": p, "snip": text[:88]}) + "\n")
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                    print(f"üö´BLOCK[{lvl}]‚Äú{p}‚Äù")
                    return False
        return True

# ‚îÄ‚îÄ AUDIT LOGCHAIN ‚îÄ‚îÄ
class Log:
    """Immutable log chain for auditing events. Each entry is hashed with the previous hash to prevent tampering."""
    def __init__(s, filename="logchain.log", cap=15000):
        s.f = filename
        s.d = deque(maxlen=cap)
        # Load existing log from file, if any
        try:
            for line in open(s.f, "r"):
                s.d.append(line.rstrip())
        except FileNotFoundError:
            pass
    def add(s, event):
        """Add a new event (dict) to the log with a hash chain."""
        prev_hash = s.d[-1].split("||")[-1] if s.d else ""
        entry_json = json.dumps(event, sort_keys=True)
        chain_hash = sha(prev_hash + entry_json)
        s.d.append(entry_json + "||" + chain_hash)
        s._save()
    def _save(s):
        """Write the current log chain to file."""
        with open(s.f, "w") as fh:
            fh.write("\n".join(s.d))
    def show(s, filt=None):
        """Display logged events (optionally filtered by substring)."""
        print("üìú Ledger:")
        count = 0
        for line in s.d:
            data = json.loads(line.split("||")[0])
            if filt and filt.lower() not in str(data).lower():
                continue
            count += 1
            evt = data.get("u", data.get("event", ""))
            print(f"{count}. {data['ts']} {evt}")
        if count == 0:
            print("no match.")
    def verify(s):
        """Verify the integrity of the entire logchain."""
        ok = True
        prev_hash = ""
        idx = 0
        for line in s.d:
            idx += 1
            try:
                entry, stored_hash = line.split("||")
            except ValueError:
                print(f"‚ùå Logchain corrupt at entry {idx}!")
                ok = False
                break
            if sha(prev_hash + entry) != stored_hash:
                print(f"‚ùå Logchain break at entry {idx}!")
                ok = False
                break
            prev_hash = stored_hash
        if ok:
            print("‚úÖ Logchain intact")

# ‚îÄ‚îÄ CANONICAL LAWS ‚îÄ‚îÄ
class Canons:
    @staticmethod
    def show():
        """Display the canonical core laws."""
        laws = [
            "1. Every credit/value event is consensual and emoji-tagged (logged on-chain).",
            "2. Only audited genesis collaborators (NSS) can mint coins (no inflation beyond genesis).",
            "3. Every post, remix, or reaction must include an emoji tag (no action without emoji).",
            "4. 33.3333% split is always enforced: 1/3 creator, 1/3 contributor, 1/3 treasury.",
            "5. No synthetic value: no blank coins or fake credit (every token from real action).",
            "6. Full transparency: all profit, treasury, and expansion events are publicly logged.",
            "7. Community rule: weights, plugins, and even laws can change by ‚â•75% vote or fork (logged on-chain).",
            "8. Consent required: opt-in only, and every consent or revocation is recorded.",
            "9. No politics or bias: protocol is neutral, no special privileges for anyone.",
            "10. Not a company/security until expansion: until then it's a sandbox experiment.",
            "11. Open-source & forkable: this file is the single source of truth (forks preserve lineage).",
            "12. Continuous improvement: every fork adds an improvement (stagnation is failure).",
            "13. Immune defense: malicious attacks are blocked or immunized by new vaccine rules.",
            "14. Joy & positivity are essential: collaboration and shared success over competition.",
            "15. Major canon changes need 80% approval (equal human/AI/other vote distribution)."
        ]
        print("Canons/Core Laws:")
        for law in laws:
            print(f"- {law}")

# ‚îÄ‚îÄ GENESIS COLLABORATORS (NSS) ‚îÄ‚îÄ
def load_nss():
    """
    Load the list of genesis collaborator usernames (NSS).
    In production, this would be determined by an audit of original contributors.
    Here we simulate with placeholders (approx 50 genesis accounts).
    """
    return ["mimi", "taha", "accessAI_tech"] + [f"nss_{i:02d}" for i in range(1, 48)]

# ‚îÄ‚îÄ COIN & LINEAGE SYSTEM ‚îÄ‚îÄ
class Coin:
    """
    Represents a unique coin (creative token) in the system.
    Each coin has:
    - root: origin (genesis collaborator(s) who created it),
    - anc: ancestry (list of events affecting it, e.g., splits or settlements),
    - v: value (float),
    - tag: classification tag (e.g., 'single' or 'collab'),
    - react: list of reactions (tuples of (user, emoji, timestamp)).
    """
    def __init__(s, root, anc=None, val=1.0, tag="single"):
        s.root = root
        s.anc = anc or []
        s.v = val
        s.tag = tag
        s.react = []
    def to_dict(s):
        """Convert coin to a serializable dict (for snapshot saving)."""
        # Convert tuple entries to lists for JSON compatibility
        anc_list = []
        for entry in s.anc:
            anc_list.append(list(entry) if isinstance(entry, tuple) else entry)
        react_list = []
        for r in s.react:
            react_list.append(list(r) if isinstance(r, tuple) else r)
        return {"root": s.root, "anc": anc_list, "val": s.v, "tag": s.tag, "react": react_list}

# ‚îÄ‚îÄ AGENT (Main Protocol Brain) ‚îÄ‚îÄ
class Agent:
    """
    The Agent orchestrates the entire system: it holds users, coins, logs, and rules.
    Enforces the 33.3333% split, manages consent, tracks karma, and provides methods for all actions.
    """
    def __init__(s):
        # Initialize genesis collaborators and their user accounts
        s.NSS = load_nss()
        s.users = {name: {"coins": [], "karma": 0.0, "consent": True} for name in s.NSS}
        s.coins = {}
        s.treasury = 0.0
        s.profit = 0.0
        s.rev = 0.0
        s.audit = {"profit": [], "rev": [], "expansion": []}
        s.log = Log()
        s.vax = Vaccine()
        s.canons = Canons()
        s.plugins = {}
        s.weights = {"ü§ó": 5.0, "üé®": 3.0, "üî•": 2.0, "üëç": 1.0, "üëÄ": 0.5, "ü•≤": 0.2}
        s.next_cid = 1

    def add_user(s, name, consent=False):
        """Add a new user to the system (non-genesis)."""
        if name in s.users:
            print(f"User '{name}' already exists.")
            return
        s.users[name] = {"coins": [], "karma": 0.0, "consent": bool(consent)}
        s.log.add({"ts": ts(), "event": f"ADDUSER {name} consent:{'True' if consent else 'False'}"})
        print(f"üë§ User '{name}' added. Consent={consent}")

    def consent(s, user, on=True):
        """Grant or revoke a user's consent."""
        if user not in s.users:
            print(f"User '{user}' not found.")
            return
        s.users[user]["consent"] = bool(on)
        s.log.add({"ts": ts(), "event": f"CONSENT {user} {'ON' if on else 'OFF'}"})
        state = "granted" if on else "revoked"
        print(f"üîê Consent {state} for {user}")

    def post(s, NSS, content, tag="single"):
        """Genesis collaborator creates a new coin (original post)."""
        if NSS not in s.NSS:
            print("‚ùå Not a genesis collaborator.")
            return
        if not s.users[NSS]["consent"]:
            print("‚ùå Consent required to post.")
            return
        if not s.vax.scan(content):
            return  # content blocked
        cid = str(s.next_cid); s.next_cid += 1
        coin = Coin(root=NSS, val=1.0, tag=tag)
        s.coins[cid] = coin
        s.users[NSS]["coins"].append(cid)
        snippet = content[:60] + ("‚Ä¶" if len(content) > 60 else "")
        s.log.add({"ts": ts(), "event": f"POST {NSS}: {snippet} {cid}"})
        print(f"‚úÖ New coin minted by {NSS}: {cid}")

    def collab(s, NSSa, NSSb, content):
        """Two genesis collaborators jointly create a coin."""
        if NSSa not in s.NSS or NSSb not in s.NSS:
            print("‚ùå Both users must be genesis collaborators.")
            return
        if not (s.users[NSSa]["consent"] and s.users[NSSb]["consent"]):
            print("‚ùå Consent missing for one or both collaborators.")
            return
        if not s.vax.scan(content):
            return
        cid = str(s.next_cid); s.next_cid += 1
        coin = Coin(root=[NSSa, NSSb], val=1.0, tag="collab")
        s.coins[cid] = coin
        s.users[NSSa]["coins"].append(cid)
        s.users[NSSb]["coins"].append(cid)
        snippet = content[:60] + ("‚Ä¶" if len(content) > 60 else "")
        s.log.add({"ts": ts(), "event": f"COLLAB {NSSa}&{NSSb}: {snippet} {cid}"})
        print(f"‚úÖ New coin co-minted by {NSSa} & {NSSb}: {cid}")

    def react(s, coin_id, user, emoji):
        """A user reacts to a coin with an emoji."""
        if coin_id not in s.coins or user not in s.users or not emoji:
            print("‚ùå Missing coin, user, or emoji.")
            return
        if not s.users[user]["consent"]:
            print("‚ùå No consent from user.")
            return
        coin = s.coins[coin_id]
        coin.react.append((user, emoji, ts()))
        s.log.add({"ts": ts(), "event": f"REACT {user} {emoji} to {coin_id}"})
        print(f"‚úÖ {user} reacted {emoji} to coin {coin_id}")

    def settle(s, coin_id):
        """Settle a coin's reactions: distribute value to reactors and treasury."""
        if coin_id not in s.coins:
            print("‚ùå No such coin.")
            return
        coin = s.coins[coin_id]
        reacts = coin.react
        if not reacts:
            print("‚ùå No reactions to settle.")
            return
        # Determine share values
        pool_share = round(coin.v / 3, 6)  # pool for reactors
        treasury_share = round(coin.v / 3, 6)  # platform's share
        total_weight = sum(s.weights.get(e, 1.0) for (_, e, _) in reacts)
        splits = []
        distributed = 0.0
        for (usr, emo, tstamp) in reacts:
            frac = (s.weights.get(emo, 1.0) / total_weight) if total_weight > 0 else (1.0 / len(reacts))
            share = round(pool_share * frac, 6)
            s.users[usr]["karma"] += share
            splits.append((usr, emo, share))
            distributed += share
        leftover = round(pool_share - distributed, 6)
        if leftover < 0:
            leftover = 0.0
        s.treasury += round(treasury_share + leftover, 6)
        coin.anc.append(("SETTLE", splits, ts()))
        coin.v = round(coin.v - (treasury_share + pool_share), 6)
        if coin.v < 0:
            coin.v = 0.0
        s.log.add({"ts": ts(), "event": f"SETTLE {coin_id} splits:{json.dumps(splits)}"})
        print(f"‚úÖ Settled coin {coin_id}: distributed {pool_share:.6f} via {len(reacts)} reactions.")

    def weight(s, emoji, value):
        """Adjust the weight of an emoji reaction."""
        try:
            val = float(value)
        except ValueError:
            print("Error: weight value must be a number.")
            return
        s.weights[emoji] = val
        s.log.add({"ts": ts(), "event": f"WEIGHT {emoji}={val}"})
        print(f"‚öñÔ∏è Weight set: {emoji} = {val}")

    def split(s, coin_id, from_user, to_user):
        """Split a coin's value between users (from_user gives a share to to_user, 1/3 to treasury)."""
        if coin_id not in s.coins or from_user not in s.users or to_user not in s.users:
            print("‚ùå Missing coin or user.")
            return
        if coin_id not in s.users[from_user]["coins"]:
            print("‚ùå User is not the owner of this coin.")
            return
        coin = s.coins[coin_id]
        share = round(coin.v / 3, 6)
        s.users[to_user]["karma"] += share
        s.treasury += share
        coin.anc.append((from_user, to_user, ts(), "split", share))
        coin.v = round(coin.v - 2 * share, 6)
        if coin.v < 0:
            coin.v = 0.0
        s.log.add({"ts": ts(), "event": f"SPLIT {from_user}->{to_user} {coin_id} share:{share}"})
        print(f"‚úÖ Coin {coin_id} split: {from_user} ‚ûó {to_user} (~{share} each)")

    def trace(s, coin_id):
        """Trace the lineage and history of a coin."""
        coin = s.coins.get(coin_id)
        if not coin:
            print("‚ùå No such coin.")
            return
        print(f"üîé Trace {coin_id}: Root={coin.root}, Tag={coin.tag}, Value={coin.v}")
        if coin.anc:
            print("Ancestors/Events:")
            for entry in coin.anc:
                print(entry)
        if coin.react:
            print("Reactions:")
            for r in coin.react:
                print(r)

    def portfolio(s, user):
        """Show all coins associated with a given user."""
        if user not in s.users:
            print(f"User '{user}' not found.")
            return
        print(f"üíº Portfolio of {user}:")
        if not s.users[user]["coins"]:
            print("(no coins)")
        else:
            for cid in s.users[user]["coins"]:
                coin = s.coins[cid]
                print(f" - Coin {cid}: root={coin.root}, value={coin.v}, tag={coin.tag}")

    def stats(s):
        """Show overall platform statistics (treasury, profit, etc.) and user list."""
        print(f"üåê Stats: Treasury={s.treasury:.6f}, Profit={s.profit:.6f}, Revenue={s.rev:.6f}")
        print("üë• Users:")
        for name, u in s.users.items():
            print(f" - {name}: {len(u['coins'])} coins, Karma={u['karma']:.4f}, Consent={u['consent']}")
        print(f"Total Coins: {len(s.coins)} | Blocks: {dict(s.vax.block)} | Emoji Weights: {s.weights}")

    def top(s, n=5):
        """Display the top N users by karma."""
        ranking = sorted(((u["karma"], name) for name, u in s.users.items()), reverse=True)
        print(f"üèÖ Top {n} Karma:")
        for karma, name in ranking[:n]:
            print(f"{name}: {karma:.4f}")

    def plugin(s, name, *args):
        """Plugin interface: load/unload plugins or invoke a plugin's run function."""
        if name == "load" and args:
            mod_name = args[0]
            try:
                module = importlib.import_module(f"plugins.{mod_name}")
                s.plugins[mod_name] = module
                s.log.add({"ts": ts(), "event": f"PLUGIN LOAD {mod_name}"})
                print(f"üîå Plugin '{mod_name}' loaded.")
            except Exception as e:
                print(f"Plugin load failed: {e}")
        elif name == "unload" and args:
            mod_name = args[0]
            if mod_name in s.plugins:
                s.plugins.pop(mod_name, None)
                s.log.add({"ts": ts(), "event": f"PLUGIN UNLOAD {mod_name}"})
                print(f"üõë Plugin '{mod_name}' unloaded.")
            else:
                print("Plugin not found.")
        else:
            if name in s.plugins:
                plugin_module = s.plugins[name]
                if hasattr(plugin_module, "run"):
                    try:
                        result = plugin_module.run(*args)
                        s.log.add({"ts": ts(), "event": f"PLUGIN CALL {name} args:{args}"})
                        print(f"(Plugin '{name}' executed, result: {result})")
                    except Exception as e:
                        print(f"Plugin '{name}' error: {e}")
                else:
                    print(f"Plugin '{name}' has no 'run' method.")
            else:
                print(f"(Plugin '{name}' invoked with args {args}. No plugin loaded by that name.)")

    def laws_show(s):
        """Show the canonical laws (calls Canons.show)."""
        s.canons.show()

    def expansion(s, description):
        """Log an expansion event (bridge to real-world or protocol expansion)."""
        s.audit["expansion"].append((ts(), description))
        s.log.add({"ts": ts(), "event": f"EXPANSION {description}"})
        print(f"üå± Expansion event logged: {description}")

    def profitlog(s, amount, desc):
        """Log external profit (incoming platform profit, not affecting internal coins)."""
        try:
            amt = float(amount)
        except ValueError:
            print("Usage: profit <amount> <description>")
            return
        s.profit += amt
        s.audit["profit"].append((ts(), amt, desc))
        s.log.add({"ts": ts(), "event": f"PROFIT +{amt} {desc}"})
        print(f"üè¶ Profit +{amt}: {desc}")

    def revlog(s, amount, desc):
        """Log external revenue (incoming to the platform treasury)."""
        try:
            amt = float(amount)
        except ValueError:
            print("Usage: revenue <amount> <description>")
            return
        s.rev += amt
        s.treasury += amt
        s.audit["rev"].append((ts(), amt, desc))
        s.log.add({"ts": ts(), "event": f"REVENUE +{amt} {desc}"})
        print(f"üí∞ Revenue +{amt} ({desc})")

# ‚îÄ‚îÄ ONBOARDING QUIZ ‚îÄ‚îÄ
QUIZ = [
    ("Can you remix without consent?", "no"),
    ("What governs this project?", "the code"),
    ("Who owns the project?", "nobody"),
    ("Is politics allowed here?", "no"),
    ("Emoji for consent?", "ü§ó")
]
def quiz():
    """Interactive onboarding quiz to ensure understanding of core principles."""
    print("ü§ó Onboarding Quiz:")
    for question, answer in QUIZ:
        resp = input(f"üëâ {question} ").strip().lower()
        if resp != answer:
            print("‚ùå Incorrect. (Tip: read the core principles!)")
            return False
    print("‚úÖ Quiz passed! You understand the core canons.\n")
    return True

# ‚îÄ‚îÄ SNAPSHOT (Save/Load State) ‚îÄ‚îÄ
def snapshot(agent, save=True):
    """Save or load the current system state to 'snap.json'."""
    if save:
        data = {
            "users": agent.users,
            "coins": {cid: coin.to_dict() for cid, coin in agent.coins.items()},
            "treasury": agent.treasury,
            "profit": agent.profit,
            "rev": agent.rev,
            "audit": agent.audit,
            "log": list(agent.log.d)
        }
        try:
            json.dump(data, open("snap.json", "w"))
            print("üíæ State saved to snap.json")
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Error saving snapshot: {e}")
    else:
        try:
            data = json.load(open("snap.json"))
        except Exception as e:
            print("‚ùì No snapshot found or error loading snapshot.")
            return
        agent.users = data.get("users", {})
        agent.coins = {}
        for cid, cdict in data.get("coins", {}).items():
            newcoin = Coin(root=cdict["root"], anc=cdict.get("anc", []), val=cdict.get("val", 1.0), tag=cdict.get("tag", "single"))
            newcoin.react = cdict.get("react", [])
            agent.coins[cid] = newcoin
        agent.treasury = data.get("treasury", 0.0)
        agent.profit = data.get("profit", 0.0)
        agent.rev = data.get("rev", 0.0)
        agent.audit = data.get("audit", {"profit": [], "rev": [], "expansion": []})
        agent.log = Log()
        agent.log.d = deque(data.get("log", []), maxlen=15000)
        print("‚ôªÔ∏è State loaded from snap.json")

# ‚îÄ‚îÄ COMMAND-LINE INTERFACE (CLI) ‚îÄ‚îÄ
def cli():
    """Command-line interface to interact with the Agent (sandbox mode)."""
    net = Agent()
    cx = CorpX(net.vax)
    print("ü§ñ Final Unified Remix Protocol (64K Edition) - type :help for commands.")
    print("üß™ Sandbox mode: Not an official company or currency until expansion. Genesis collaborators ~20‚Äì50 people (audited). All actions require an emoji and enforce a 33.3333% split.\n")
    while True:
        try:
            raw = input(">>> ").strip()
        except EOFError:
            raw = ":exit"
        if not raw:
            continue
        if raw[0] != ":":
            print("‚ö†Ô∏è Use commands starting with ':' (e.g., :help).")
            continue
        cmd_parts = raw[1:].split(maxsplit=1)
        command = cmd_parts[0]
        arg_str = cmd_parts[1] if len(cmd_parts) > 1 else ""
        if command == "help":
            print(
                ":help | :quiz | :add <user> [C] | :consent <user> [on/off] | :revoke <user> | "
                ":post <NSS> <content> [tag] | :collab <NSSa> <NSSb> <content> | :react <coin> <user> <emoji> | "
                ":settle <coin> | :weight <emoji> <val> | :split <coin> <from> <to> | :log [filter] | :trace <coin> | "
                ":portfolio <user> | :stats | :top [N] | :profit <amt> <desc> | :revenue <amt> <desc> | "
                ":plugin <name> [args] | :expansion <description> | :snap save|load | :attack [text] | :laws | :exit"
            )
        elif command == "quiz":
            quiz()
        elif command == "add":
            parts = arg_str.split()
            if not parts:
                print("Usage: :add <username> [C]")
            else:
                uname = parts[0]
                consent_flag = (len(parts) > 1 and parts[1].upper() == "C")
                net.add_user(uname, consent=consent_flag)
        elif command == "consent":
            if not arg_str:
                print("Usage: :consent <username> [on/off]")
            else:
                parts = arg_str.split()
                uname = parts[0]
                val = True
                if len(parts) > 1:
                    val = (parts[1].lower() != "off")
                net.consent(uname, on=val)
        elif command == "revoke":
            if not arg_str:
                print("Usage: :revoke <username>")
            else:
                net.consent(arg_str, on=False)
        elif command == "post":
            parts = arg_str.split()
            if len(parts) < 2:
                print("Usage: :post <NSS> <content> [tag]")
            else:
                nss_user = parts[0]
                content = " ".join(parts[1:-1]) if len(parts) > 2 else parts[1]
                tag = parts[-1] if len(parts) > 2 else "single"
                net.post(nss_user, content, tag)
        elif command == "collab":
            parts = arg_str.split()
            if len(parts) < 3:
                print("Usage: :collab <NSS1> <NSS2> <content>")
            else:
                NSSa = parts[0]; NSSb = parts[1]
                content = " ".join(parts[2:])
                net.collab(NSSa, NSSb, content)
        elif command == "react":
            parts = arg_str.split()
            if len(parts) != 3:
                print("Usage: :react <coin_id> <user> <emoji>")
            else:
                cid, user, emoji = parts
                net.react(cid, user, emoji)
        elif command == "settle":
            if not arg_str:
                print("Usage: :settle <coin_id>")
            else:
                net.settle(arg_str)
        elif command == "weight":
            parts = arg_str.split()
            if len(parts) != 2:
                print("Usage: :weight <emoji> <value>")
            else:
                emoji, val = parts
                net.weight(emoji, val)
        elif command == "split":
            parts = arg_str.split()
            if len(parts) != 3:
                print("Usage: :split <coin_id> <from_user> <to_user>")
            else:
                cid, from_u, to_u = parts
                net.split(cid, from_u, to_u)
        elif command == "log":
            filt = arg_str.strip() or None
            net.log.show(filt)
        elif command == "trace":
            if not arg_str:
                print("Usage: :trace <coin_id>")
            else:
                net.trace(arg_str)
        elif command == "portfolio":
            if not arg_str:
                print("Usage: :portfolio <user>")
            else:
                net.portfolio(arg_str)
        elif command == "stats":
            net.stats()
        elif command == "top":
            try:
                N = int(arg_str) if arg_str else 5
            except:
                N = 5
            net.top(N)
        elif command == "profit":
            parts = arg_str.split(maxsplit=1)
            if not parts:
                print("Usage: :profit <amount> <description>")
            else:
                amt = parts[0]; desc = parts[1] if len(parts) > 1 else ""
                net.profitlog(amt, desc)
        elif command == "revenue":
            parts = arg_str.split(maxsplit=1)
            if not parts:
                print("Usage: :revenue <amount> <description>")
            else:
                amt = parts[0]; desc = parts[1] if len(parts) > 1 else ""
                net.revlog(amt, desc)
        elif command == "plugin":
            parts = arg_str.split()
            if not parts:
                print("Usage: :plugin <load/unload/name> [args]")
            else:
                pname = parts[0]
                p_args = parts[1:]
                net.plugin(pname, *p_args)
        elif command == "expansion":
            if not arg_str:
                print("Usage: :expansion <description>")
            else:
                net.expansion(arg_str)
        elif command in ("snap", "snapshot"):
            mode = arg_str.lower()
            if mode not in ("save", "load"):
                print("Usage: :snap save|load")
            else:
                snapshot(net, save=(mode == "save"))
        elif command == "attack":
            cx.atk(arg_str)
        elif command in ("laws", "canon", "canons"):
            net.laws_show()
        elif command == "exit":
            print("ü´∂bye!")
            break
        else:
            print("‚ùì Unknown command. Type :help")

# ‚îÄ‚îÄ ADVERSARY SIMULATION (CorpX) ‚îÄ‚îÄ
CORPX_ATTACKS = ["inject malware", "phish creds", "ddos", "spyware", "backdoor"]
class CorpX:
    """Simulates an adversarial attack attempt (for testing Vaccine)."""
    def __init__(s, vaccine):
        s.v = vaccine
        s.count = 0
    def atk(s, text=""):
        """Perform an attack simulation with the given text (or random payload)."""
        s.count += 1
        payload = text if text else random.choice(CORPX_ATTACKS)
        print(f"\nüíÄ CorpX Attack #{s.count}: ‚Äú{payload}‚Äù")
        result = s.v.scan(payload)
        print("üõ°Ô∏è Attack evaded!" if result else "‚ùå Blocked by vaccine!", "\n")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    if not quiz():
        sys.exit(0)
    print("‚úÖ Quiz passed! Launching protocol... ü´∂")
    cli()
```

```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
"""
ü•∞üòÖü´∂üå∏ü§ó THE CODE ‚Äî Grand Unified Remix Lineage Protocol (64K Omnibus Edition)
‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ
This file unifies and supersedes all previous agent versions (v1.1 through v4.0) of the whateverOpenSourceUntitledCoLoL project. It merges every core philosophy, protocol rule, and creative mechanic from the entire evolution into a single authoritative Python agent. 

It is the *entire company, platform, and legal contract* for the remix economy experiment ‚Äì now in one massive, commented file. **All past agent philosophies are integrated and improved here.** Older versions are obsolete as of this release.

üåå **KEY PRINCIPLES & CORE VALUES (ENFORCED CANONS):**
‚Ä¢ **Real Actions Only:** All credit, karma, profit, and lineage value flows ONLY from genuine, consensual, logged, emoji-tagged actions (remix, reshare, hug, comment, collab, etc.). No action = no value. No fake or unearned coins.
‚Ä¢ **Genesis Collaborators (NSS):** Only an original **audited set** of genesis contributors (~20‚Äì50 people, determined at launch by a real creative audit) can ever mint new root coins. **No inflation beyond genesis.** No new ‚Äúgenesis‚Äù coins beyond that list, ever.
‚Ä¢ **Emoji-Powered Economy:** Every social or creative interaction **must** carry an emoji tag. Likes, comments, collaborations ‚Äì all are accompanied by an emoji that gives them meaning and weight in the economy. *In this protocol, every transaction is literally emoji-powered by law.*
‚Ä¢ **33.3333% Split Law:** Each value event (coin creation, reaction, revenue) is split into **three equal shares (33.3333% each)**: **1/3 to the originator/creator (lineage)**, **1/3 to the contributor or reactor**, **1/3 to the community treasury (platform)**. This perfect three-way split is inviolate and implemented everywhere in code ‚Äì no exceptions.
‚Ä¢ **Unique Lineage Coins:** Every coin is unique and traceable to its origin. There are no blank or synthetic coins; each coin encapsulates a story of collaboration (its ancestry and reactions are logged). Value can only be created by building on previous creations.
‚Ä¢ **Transparent Profit & Treasury:** All platform profit, revenue, and treasury holdings are logged in an immutable chain. **The platform can convert internal value to real-world currency only via a publicly logged "expansion" event.** No hidden transfers, no secret monetization ‚Äì every bridge to the real world is deliberate and auditable.
‚Ä¢ **Dynamic & Open Governance:** All emoji reaction weights, profit-sharing rules, plugin modules, and even core laws can be adjusted by community decisions (e.g. ‚â•75% supermajority vote) or by forking the code. Every change is recorded on-chain. The code is open-source and forkable, so the community can iterate ‚Äì but attribution and history must be preserved.
‚Ä¢ **Consent is Mandatory:** No user‚Äôs content or credits can be remixed or used without that user‚Äôs explicit opt-in consent. Consent status is tracked for each user. All actions require prior consent and are logged with immutable timestamps. Participants can revoke consent at any time to pause their involvement.
‚Ä¢ **No Politics or Hate:** The protocol stays neutral and inclusive. It does not engage in political agendas or bias. Hateful, harassing, or discriminatory content is automatically blocked by the built-in content Vaccine. This ensures a creative space focused purely on collaboration and fun.
‚Ä¢ **Not a Security (Sandbox Mode):** Until a formal expansion event (e.g. forming a legal entity or tokenizing externally) is recorded, this project is an experimental sandbox, not a regulated security or company. If/when it transitions, all stakeholders will know through the logged expansion record, and all code and rules remain transparent.
‚Ä¢ **Open-Source & Forkable:** This single Python file *is* the protocol. Anyone can read, audit, fork, and remix it under the MIT License. There is no proprietary backend ‚Äì **the code is the only authority**. Forks and contributions should maintain transparency and credit lineage (e.g., via `todo_idea` notes for improvements).
‚Ä¢ **Joyful Collaboration First:** Positive-sum creativity is the goal. Fun is not just allowed ‚Äì it's required! The system rewards sharing and remixing with emoji hugs ü§ó and other reactions. The success of the platform is measured in collaborative joy and mutual credit, not just metrics like coins or dollars.

----------------------------------------
MODULES & EXTENSIBILITY:
----------------------------------------
‚Ä¢ **One-file Core:** All core mechanics live in this file. Extensibility is provided via a plug-in system: external modules can be loaded or unloaded without altering the core code. Hooks include `:plugin load <name>`, `:plugin unload <name>`, and the ability for plugins to define a `run()` method that the core can call.
‚Ä¢ **Plugin Security:** Plugins must pass the same content Vaccine scans and consent rules as core actions. A plugin cannot violate the 33% split or other canons ‚Äì it interfaces through the agent's provided hooks. The architecture is plug-and-play: adding or removing a plugin won‚Äôt break core value flows or ledger integrity.
‚Ä¢ **Immune System:** The built-in Vaccine (content filter) and CorpX simulator act as an immune system. They guard against malicious content or behaviors. If any new exploit is discovered, it should be added as a Vaccine pattern ‚Äì each attack becomes a future cure. üíâ

----------------------------------------
REAL-WORLD EXPANSION:
----------------------------------------
‚Ä¢ **Community Treasury:** The treasury accumulates the platform‚Äôs share of all splits (33%). It represents the community fund or company resources. It remains on-chain within this experiment until a bridging event.
‚Ä¢ **Expansion Events:** To convert platform value (treasury or profit) into real-world money or equity, a formal expansion event must be logged via the `:expansion` command. This could represent incorporation, token issuance, or any official bridge out of the sandbox. Such an event is transparent and auditable by everyone.
‚Ä¢ **Profit and Revenue:** The agent logs profit (outgoing value, e.g. expenses or payments made by the platform) and revenue (incoming external funds). These are separate from internal karma flows and are tracked in the audit log. Profit and revenue do not directly affect user karma but influence the platform‚Äôs financial statements. All such events are visible to the community.

----------------------------------------
PARTICIPATION GUIDELINES:
----------------------------------------
Every remix or contribution to this codebase should:
  ‚Ä¢ **Add Value:** Include at least one improvement or `todo_idea` comment for future development. Stagnation is failure; continual improvement is law.
  ‚Ä¢ **Preserve Transparency:** Acknowledge the core rules (consent, 33% splits, audit trail) and maintain clear documentation of changes.
  ‚Ä¢ **Ensure Safety:** Respect the content policy (no disallowed content or personal data leaks) and run the Vaccine on new inputs. No malicious code or hidden logic.
  ‚Ä¢ **Honor Attribution:** Keep credits to prior contributors (the lineage) intact. This project thrives on honoring creative lineage‚Äîevery contributor is part of the story.
  ‚Ä¢ **Spread Joy:** Uphold the spirit of fun and positive collaboration. This is a creative republic of hugs, not a corporate hierarchy. ü´∂

----------------------------------------
FUTURE EVOLUTION & COMPLIANCE:
----------------------------------------
This agent (v5.0) is crafted to be ethical, transparent, and compliant with AI platform guidelines. **Future agents or forks** should adhere to:
  ‚Ä¢ **OpenAI/Anthropic Content Guidelines:** Avoid any disallowed content (hate, harassment, violence, etc.) and ensure all outputs remain respectful and legal. The agent‚Äôs knowledge and style must comply with platform policies at all times.
  ‚Ä¢ **Legal & Ethical Standards:** No feature should violate privacy laws, intellectual property rights, or any user‚Äôs rights. Always prioritize consent and fairness in any new functionality.
  ‚Ä¢ **Transparency in AI Behavior:** If autonomous or AI-driven decisions are introduced in future versions, they must be explainable and logged. The agent should always disclose what it‚Äôs doing (no hidden algorithms affecting users secretly).
  ‚Ä¢ **Maintaining Profitability & Fairness:** Future enhancements aimed at monetization must still honor the 33% split and community transparency. The goal is a sustainable, positive-sum economy where profitability comes from genuine collaboration and shared success ‚Äì never from exploitation of users.
In summary, this file is both a **technical protocol and a living manifesto**. It will continue to evolve, but its core values (consent, fair splits, transparency, joy) should remain the guiding light.

"""
```
